         #How to remount /etc/fstab without rebooting
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <a id="How_to_mount_Windows_partitions_.28FAT.29_on_boot-up.2C_and_allow_all_users_to_read.2Fwrite" name="How_to_mount_Windows_partitions_.28FAT.29_on_boot-up.2C_and_allow_all_users_to_read.2Fwrite">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to mount Windows partitions (FAT) on boot-up, and allow all users to read/write
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_list_partition_tables" title="">
         #How to list partition tables
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <i>
         e.g. Assumed that /dev/hda1 is the location of Windows partition (FAT)
        </i>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        <i>
         Local mount folder: /media/windows
        </i>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <pre>
       mkdir /media/windows
cp /etc/fstab /etc/fstab_backup
gedit /etc/fstab
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Append the following line at the end of file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       /dev/hda1    /media/windows vfat  iocharset=utf8,umask=000  0    0
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Save the edited file
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_remount_.2Fetc.2Ffstab_without_rebooting" title="">
         #How to remount /etc/fstab without rebooting
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <a id="Security" name="Security">
      </a>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        Security
       </span>
      </h2>
      <a id="What_are_the_basic_things_I_need_to_know_about_securing_my_Fedora" name="What_are_the_basic_things_I_need_to_know_about_securing_my_Fedora">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        What are the basic things I need to know about securing my Fedora
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Ensure hard drive is first in BIOS boot-up sequence
        <ul>
         <li>
          To prevent trespassers from using Linux Installation CD which allows them to gain root user access
         </li>
         <li>
          To prevent trespassers from using Linux Live CD (e.g. Fedora/KNOPPIX/MEPIS) which allows them to destroy/browse/share the entire hard drive
         </li>
         <li>
          To prevent trespassers from installing another Operating System
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
       <li>
        Ensure a password is set for BIOS
        <ul>
         <li>
          To prevent trespassers from changing the BIOS boot-up sequence
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
       <li>
        Ensure computer is located at a secured place
        <ul>
         <li>
          To prevent trespassers from removing computer's hard drive which allows them to destroy/browse/share the entire hard drive from a different computer
         </li>
         <li>
          To prevent trespassers from removing computer's on-board battery which resets the BIOS password
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
       <li>
        Ensure passwords used on the system cannot be easily guessed
        <ul>
         <li>
          To prevent trespassers from cracking password file using brute force attacks (e.g. John the Ripper)
         </li>
         <li>
          Create password with minimum length of 8 characters
         </li>
         <li>
          Create password with mixture of characters/numbers, and upper/lower case
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
       <li>
        Ensure interactive editing control for GRUB menu is disabled
        <ul>
         <li>
          To prevent trespassers from modifying kernel boot-up arguments which allows them to have root user access
         </li>
         <li>
          Read
          <a href="#How_to_disable_all_interactive_editing_control_for_GRUB_menu" title="">
           #How to disable all interactive editing control for GRUB menu
          </a>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
       <li>
        Ensure history listing is disabled in Console mode
        <ul>
         <li>
          To prevent trespassers from seeing previously issued commands
         </li>
         <li>
          Read
          <a href="#How_to_disable_history_listing_in_Console_mode" title="">
           #How to disable history listing in Console mode
          </a>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
       <li>
        Ensure Ctrl+Alt+Del is disabled in Console mode
        <ul>
         <li>
          To prevent trespassers from restarting the system without permission in Console mode
         </li>
         <li>
          Read
          <a href="#How_to_disable_Ctrl.2BAlt.2BDel_from_restarting_computer_in_Console_mode" title="">
           #How to disable Ctrl+Alt+Del from restarting computer in Console mode
          </a>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
       <li>
        Ensure interactive option is set for remove, copy and move of files/folders in Console mode
        <ul>
         <li>
          To prevent accidental removal/overwritten of files/folders
         </li>
         <li>
          Read
          <a href="#How_to_enable_prompt_before_removal.2Foverwritten_of_files.2Ffolders_in_Console_mode" title="">
           #How to enable prompt before removal/overwritten of files/folders in Console mode
          </a>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
       <li>
        For day to day usage, login as a normal user
        <ul>
         <li>
          To prevent accidental deletion/modification of system files/folders
         </li>
         <li>
          Read
          <a href="#How_to_add.2Fedit.2Fdelete_system_users" title="">
           #How to add/edit/delete system users
          </a>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
       <li>
        Disable root user account, use "sudo" instead
        <ul>
         <li>
          To reduce the amount of time spent with root privileges, and thus the risk of inadvertently executing a command as root
         </li>
         <li>
          "sudo" provides a more useful audit trail (/var/log/auth.log)
         </li>
         <li>
          Read
          <a href="#How_to_disable_root_user_account" title="">
           #How to disable root user account
          </a>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
       <li>
        Install a Firewall
        <ul>
         <li>
          A firewall does not guarantee security but it is in most environments the first line of defense against network based attacks
         </li>
         <li>
          Read
          <a href="#How_to_install_Firewall_.28Firestarter.29" title="">
           #How to install Firewall (Firestarter)
          </a>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
       <li>
        Perform vulnerability test
        <ul>
         <li>
          Nessus is a great tool designed to automate the testing and discovery of known security problems
         </li>
         <li>
          Read
          <a href="#How_to_install_Vulnerability_Scanner_.28Nessus.29" title="">
           #How to install Vulnerability Scanner (Nessus)
          </a>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <a id="How_to_disable_all_interactive_editing_control_for_GRUB_menu" name="How_to_disable_all_interactive_editing_control_for_GRUB_menu">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to disable all interactive editing control for GRUB menu
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       grub
      </pre>
      <pre>
       grub&gt; md5crypt
Password: ****** (Fedora)
Encrypted: $1$ZWnke0$1fzDBVjUcT1Mpdd4u/T961 (encrypted password)
grub&gt; quit
      </pre>
      <pre>
       cp /boot/grub/menu.lst /boot/grub/menu.lst_backup
gedit /boot/grub/menu.lst
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Find this section
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       ...
## password ['--md5'] passwd
# If used in the first section of a menu file, disable all interactive editing
# control (menu entry editor and command-line) and entries protected by the
# command 'lock'
# e.g. password topsecret
#   password --md5 $1$gLhU0/$aW78kHK1QfV3P2b2znUoe/
# password topsecret
...
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Add the following line below it
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       password --md5 $1$ZWnke0$1fzDBVjUcT1Mpdd4u/T961 (encrypted password above)
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Find this section
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       ...
title		Fedora, kernel 2.6.10-5-386 (recovery mode)
root		(hd0,1)
kernel		/boot/vmlinuz-2.6.10-5-386 root=/dev/hda2 ro single
initrd		/boot/initrd.img-2.6.10-5-386
savedefault
boot
...
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Replace with the following lines
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       #title		Fedora, kernel 2.6.10-5-386 (recovery mode)
#root		(hd0,1)
#kernel		/boot/vmlinuz-2.6.10-5-386 root=/dev/hda2 ro single
#initrd		/boot/initrd.img-2.6.10-5-386
#savedefault
#boot
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Save the edited file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <a id="How_to_disable_history_listing_in_Console_mode" name="How_to_disable_history_listing_in_Console_mode">
      </a>

       rm -f $HOME/.bash_history
touch $HOME/.bash_history

      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_disable_Ctrl.2BAlt.2BDel_from_restarting_computer_in_Console_mode" name="How_to_disable_Ctrl.2BAlt.2BDel_from_restarting_computer_in_Console_mode">

       <span class="mw-headline">

      </ul>
      <pre>

      <a id="How_to_enable_prompt_before_removal.2Foverwritten_of_files.2Ffolders_in_Console_mode" name="How_to_enable_prompt_before_removal.2Foverwritten_of_files.2Ffolders_in_Console_mode">

Password: ****** (Fedora)

      <a id="Tips_.26_Tricks" name="Tips_.26_Tricks">
      </a>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        Tips &amp; Tricks
       </span>
      </h2>
      <a id="How_to_add_extra_Wallpapers.2C_Icons_and_Themes" name="How_to_add_extra_Wallpapers.2C_Icons_and_Themes">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to add extra Wallpapers, Icons and Themes
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        To add extra backgrounds
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       wget -c
       <a class="external free" href="http://easylinux.info/uploads/backgrounds.tar.gz" title="http://easylinux.info/uploads/backgrounds.tar.gz">
        http://easylinux.info/uploads/backgrounds.tar.gz
       </a>
       tar zxvf backgrounds.tar.gz -C /usr/share
rm -f backgrounds.tar.gz
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Check weather you have file
        <i>
         backgrounds.xml
        </i>
        n your
        <i>
         .gnome/
        </i>
        directory
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       ls $HOME/.gnome2/ | grep "backgrounds.xml"
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        If this line printed out "backgrounds.xml" then run
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       cp --preserve=ownership $USER_HOME/.gnome2/backgrounds.xml $USER_HOME/.gnome2/backgrounds.xml_backup
sed -n -e '1,3p' $USER_HOME/.gnome2/backgrounds.xml_backup &gt; $USER_HOME/.gnome2/backgrounds.xml
cat /usr/share/backgrounds/frog.xml &gt;&gt; $USER_HOME/.gnome2/backgrounds.xml
sed -n -e '4,$p' $USER_HOME/.gnome2/backgrounds.xml_backup &gt;&gt; $USER_HOME/.gnome2/backgrounds.xml
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        ELSE run
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       cp /usr/share/backgrounds/backgrounds.xml $USER_HOME/.gnome2/backgrounds.xml
chmod 777 $USER_HOME/.gnome2/backgrounds.xml
      </pre>
      <p>
       <br/>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        To add extra Icons and Themes run
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       wget -c
       <a class="external free" href="http://easylinux.info/uploads/icons.tar.gz" title="http://easylinux.info/uploads/icons.tar.gz">
        http://easylinux.info/uploads/icons.tar.gz
       </a>
       tar zxvf icons.tar.gz -C $USER_HOME
rm -f icons.tar.gz
wget -c
       <a class="external free" href="http://easylinux.info/uploads/themes.tar.gz" title="http://easylinux.info/uploads/themes.tar.gz">
        http://easylinux.info/uploads/themes.tar.gz
       </a>
       tar zxvf themes.tar.gz -C $USER_HOME
rm -f themes.tar.gz
      </pre>
      <p>
       <br/>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Try changing your background, and look in Applications -&gt; Preferences -&gt; Themes (Theme details)
       </li>
      </ul>
      <a id="How_to_add_the_Open_Terminal_to_the_R-Click" name="How_to_add_the_Open_Terminal_to_the_R-Click">

       </li>

      <a id="How_to_get_a_shortcut_to_Root_Terminal" name="How_to_get_a_shortcut_to_Root_Terminal">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to get a shortcut to Root Terminal
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>

        <a href="#How_to_add_extra_repositories" title="">
         #How to add extra repositories

      <a id="How_to_enable_the_.22Switch_User.22_button_on_the_GNOME_screensaver" name="How_to_enable_the_.22Switch_User.22_button_on_the_GNOME_screensaver">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to enable the "Switch User" button on the GNOME screensaver
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        To do this to just for one user
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       gconftool-2 --type bool --set /apps/gnome-screensaver/user_switch_enabled true
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        To do this for every user
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       gconftool-2 --direct --config-source xml:readwrite:/etc/gconf/gconf.xml.defaults --type bool --set /apps/gnome-screensaver/user_switch_enabled true
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_restart_GNOME_without_rebooting_computer" name="How_to_restart_GNOME_without_rebooting_computer">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to restart GNOME without rebooting computer
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Save and close all opened applications
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       Press 'Ctrl + Alt + Backspace'
      </pre>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        or
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <pre>
       /usr/sbin/gdm-restart
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_turn_on_Num_Lock_on_GNOME_startup" name="How_to_turn_on_Num_Lock_on_GNOME_startup">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to turn on Num Lock on GNOME startup
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_add_extra_repositories" title="">
         #How to add extra repositories
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       yum -y install numlockx
cp /etc/X11/gdm/Init/Default /etc/X11/gdm/Init/Default_backup
gedit /etc/X11/gdm/Init/Default
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Find this line (the last line)
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       ...
exit 0
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Add the following lines above it
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       if [ -x /usr/bin/numlockx ]; then
 /usr/bin/numlockx on
fi
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Save the edited file
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_restart_GNOME_without_rebooting_computer" title="">
         #How to restart GNOME without rebooting computer
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <a id="How_to_switch_to_Console_mode_in_GNOME" name="How_to_switch_to_Console_mode_in_GNOME">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to switch to Console mode in GNOME
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        To switch to Console mode
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       Press 'Ctrl + Alt + F1' (F2 - F6)
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        To switch between consles in Console mode
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       Press 'Alt + F1' (F2 - F6)
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        To switch back to GNOME mode
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       Press 'Alt + F7'
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_disable_Ctrl.2BAlt.2BBackspace_from_restarting_X_in_GNOME" name="How_to_disable_Ctrl.2BAlt.2BBackspace_from_restarting_X_in_GNOME">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to disable Ctrl+Alt+Backspace from restarting X in GNOME
       </span>
      </h4>

EndSection
      </pre>

       <li>

        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>

      <a id="How_to_enable_autosave_in_Gedit_and_disable_creation_of_some_file.7E_files" name="How_to_enable_autosave_in_Gedit_and_disable_creation_of_some_file.7E_files">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to enable autosave in Gedit and disable creation of some_file~ files
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Applications -&gt; System Tools -&gt; Configuration Editor
       </li>
       <li>
        Configuration Editor
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       / -&gt; apps -&gt; gedit-2 -&gt; preferences -&gt; editor -&gt; save -&gt; create_backup_copy (
       <b>
        Unchecked
       </b>
       )
/ -&gt; apps -&gt; gedit-2 -&gt; preferences -&gt; editor -&gt; save -&gt; auto_save (
       <b>
        Checked
       </b>
       )
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_show_all_hidden_files.2Ffolders_in_Nautilus" name="How_to_show_all_hidden_files.2Ffolders_in_Nautilus">

       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to show all hidden files/folders in Nautilus

       </li>

       </b>
       )
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_browse_files.2Ffolders_as_root_user_in_Nautilus" name="How_to_browse_files.2Ffolders_as_root_user_in_Nautilus">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to browse files/folders as root user in Nautilus
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_add_extra_repositories" title="">
         #How to add extra repositories
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       yum -y install gksu
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        To install File Browser (Root)
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       gedit /usr/share/applications/Nautilus-root.desktop
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <ul>
         <li>
          Insert the following lines into the new file
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       [Desktop Entry]
Name=File Browser (Root)
Comment=Browse the filesystem with the file manager
Exec=gksu "nautilus --browser ."
Icon=file-manager
Terminal=false
Type=Application
Categories=Application;System;
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <ul>
         <li>
          Save the edited file
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <ul>
       <li>
        To browse files/folders as root user in Nautilus
        <ul>
         <li>
          Applications -&gt; System Tools -&gt; File Browser (Root)
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>

       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to open files as root user via right click
       </span>
      </h4>

         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>

       gedit $HOME/.gnome2/nautilus-scripts/Open\ as\ root

       </li>

       for uri in $NAUTILUS_SCRIPT_SELECTED_URIS; do
	gnome-"gnome-open $uri" &amp;
done
      </pre>

       </li>
      </ul>

       chmod +x $HOME/.gnome2/nautilus-scripts/Open\ as\ root

       </span>

        </a>

      <a id="How_to_install.2Funinstall_.rpm_files" name="How_to_install.2Funinstall_.rpm_files">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to install/uninstall .rpm files
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        To install .rpm file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       rpm -i package_file.rpm
      </pre>

       <li>
        To uninstall .rpm file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       rpm -e package_name
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_rename_all_files_in_directory_at_once" name="How_to_rename_all_files_in_directory_at_once">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to rename all files in directory at once
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        One should NEVER install anything from source on an RPM-based distro like Fedora! The proper way to bulk-rename files is to install mmv (Multi-Move)
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       yum install mmv
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Move your files
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       mmv "*".jpg new_prefix_"#1".jpg
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        This would literally rename 1.jpg, 2.jpg and 3.jpg to new_prefix_1.jpg, new_prefix_2.jpg and new_prefix_3.jpg
       </li>
      </ul>
      <a id="How_to_manipulate_all_image_files_in_directory_at_once" name="How_to_manipulate_all_image_files_in_directory_at_once">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to manipulate all image files in directory at once
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        To install bash batch image processing script
        <ul>
         <li>
          Read
          <a href="#How_to_add_extra_repositories" title="">
           #How to add extra repositories
          </a>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       yum -y install ImageMagick
wget -c
       <a class="external free" href="http://easylinux.info/uploads/bbips.0.3.2.sh" title="http://easylinux.info/uploads/bbips.0.3.2.sh">
        http://easylinux.info/uploads/bbips.0.3.2.sh
       </a>
       cp bbips.0.3.2.sh /usr/bin/bbips
chmod 755 /usr/bin/bbips
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        To manipulate all image files in directory at once
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       bbips
      </pre>

        How to change default Operating System boot-up for GRUB menu

      <a id="How_to_display_Splash_Image_for_GRUB_menu_on_boot-up" name="How_to_display_Splash_Image_for_GRUB_menu_on_boot-up">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to display Splash Image for GRUB menu on boot-up
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <i>
         e.g. Assumed that hd0,1 is the location of Fedora boot partition
        </i>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <pre>
       wget -c
       <a class="external free" href="http://easylinux.info/uploads/fedora.xpm.gz" title="http://easylinux.info/uploads/fedora.xpm.gz">
        http://easylinux.info/uploads/fedora.xpm.gz
       </a>
       chmod 644 fedora.xpm.gz
mkdir /boot/grub/images
cp fedora.xpm.gz /boot/grub/images/
cp /boot/grub/menu.lst /boot/grub/menu.lst_backup
gedit /boot/grub/menu.lst
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Find this section
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       # menu.lst - See: grub(8), info grub, update-grub(8)
#      grub-install(8), grub-floppy(8),
#      grub-md5-crypt, /usr/share/doc/grub
#      and /usr/share/doc/grub-doc/.
...
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Add the following line below it
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       splashimage (hd0,1)/boot/grub/images/fedora.xpm.gz
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Save the edited file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <a id="How_to_convert_Wallpaper_to_Splash_Image_for_GRUB_menu" name="How_to_convert_Wallpaper_to_Splash_Image_for_GRUB_menu">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to convert Wallpaper to Splash Image for GRUB menu
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <i>
         e.g. Assumed that wallpaper.png is the Wallpaper to be converted to Splash Image
        </i>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        <i>
         splashimage.xpm.gz is the Splash Image for GRUB menu
        </i>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <pre>
       convert -resize 640x480 -colors 14 wallpaper.png splashimage.xpm &amp;&amp; gzip splashimage.xpm
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_display_Splash_Image_for_GRUB_menu_on_boot-up" title="">
         #How to display Splash Image for GRUB menu on boot-up
        </a>
        (use splashimage.xpm.gz instead of Fedora.xpm.gz)
       </li>
      </ul>

      <a id="How_to_clean_.2Ftmp.2F_folder_contents_on_shutdown" name="How_to_clean_.2Ftmp.2F_folder_contents_on_shutdown">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to clean /tmp/ folder contents on shutdown
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       cp /etc/init.d/sysklogd /etc/init.d/sysklogd_backup
gedit /etc/init.d/sysklogd
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Find this section
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       ...
 stop)
  log_begin_msg "Stopping system log daemon..."
  start-stop-daemon --stop --quiet --oknodo --exec $binpath --pidfile $pidfile
  log_end_msg $?
...
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Add the following line below it
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       rm -fr /tmp/* /tmp/.??*
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Save the edited file
       </li>
      </ul>

      <a id="How_to_remove_duplicate_menu.2Fmenu_items_in_GNOME" name="How_to_remove_duplicate_menu.2Fmenu_items_in_GNOME">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to remove duplicate menu/menu items in GNOME
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       rm -f $HOME/.config/menus/applications.menu
      </pre>
      <p>
       <br/>
      </p>
      <a id="Open_Terminal_Here_in_Nautilus" name="Open_Terminal_Here_in_Nautilus">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        Open Terminal Here in Nautilus
       </span>
      </h4>
      <pre>
       gedit ~/.gnome2/nautilus-scripts/"Open Terminal Here"
      </pre>
      <p>
       add the following text
      </p>
      <pre>
       #!/usr/bin/perl -w
use strict;
$_ = $ENV{'NAUTILUS_SCRIPT_CURRENT_URI'};
if ($_ and m#^file:///#) {
s/%([0-9A-Fa-f]{2})/chr(hex($1))/eg;
s#^file://##;
exec "gnome-terminal --working-directory='$_'";
}
# Added 2003-12-08 Dexter Ang
if ($_ == "x-nautilus-desktop:///") {
$_ = $ENV{'HOME'};
$_ = $_.'/Desktop';
exec "gnome-terminal --working-directory='$_'";
}
      </pre>
      <p>
       Save and close Gedit
      </p>
      <p>
       Right click the desktop choose Scripts  then "Open Terminal Here"
      </p>
      <p>
       <br/>
      </p>
      <a id="Open_Root_Terminal_Here_in_Naultilus" name="Open_Root_Terminal_Here_in_Naultilus">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        Open Root Terminal Here in Naultilus
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#Set_up_Sudo_on_your_PC" title="">
         #Set up Sudo on your PC
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       gedit ~/.gnome2/nautilus-scripts/"Open Root Terminal Here"
      </pre>
      <p>
       Add the following
      </p>
      <pre>
       #!/bin/sh
cd $NAUTILUS_SCRIPT_CURRENT_URI
sudo gnome-terminal
      </pre>
      <p>
       <br/>
       Save and close Gedit
      </p>
      <p>
       Right click the desktop choose Scripts then "Open Terminal Here"
      </p>
      <a id="Samba_Server" name="Samba_Server">
      </a>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        Samba Server
       </span>
      </h2>
      <a id="How_to_install_Samba_Server_for_files.2Ffolders_sharing_service" name="How_to_install_Samba_Server_for_files.2Ffolders_sharing_service">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to install Samba Server for files/folders sharing service
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_add_extra_repositories" title="">
         #How to add extra repositories
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Use
        <i>
         Desktop -&gt; System Settings -&gt; Add/Remove Applications
        </i>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <b>
         or
        </b>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <pre>
       yum -y install samba
yum -y install samba-client
yum -y install system-config-samba
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Desktop -&gt; System Settings -&gt; Server Settings -&gt; Samba
       </li>
      </ul>
      <a id="How_to_add.2Fedit.2Fdelete_network_users" name="How_to_add.2Fedit.2Fdelete_network_users">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to add/edit/delete network users
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Use
        <i>
         *Desktop -&gt; System Settings -&gt; Server Settings -&gt; Samba
        </i>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <b>
         or
        </b>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <ul>
       <li>
        To add network user
        <ul>
         <li>
          Read
          <a href="#How_to_add.2Fedit.2Fdelete_system_users" title="">
           #How to add/edit/delete system users
          </a>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       smbpasswd -a system_username
gedit /etc/samba/smbusers
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <ul>
         <li>
          Insert the following line into the new file
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       system_username = "network username"
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <ul>
         <li>
          Save the edited file
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
       <li>
        To edit network user
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       smbpasswd -a system_username
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        To delete network user
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       smbpasswd -x system_username
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_share_home_folders_with_read.2Fwrite_permissions_.28Authentication.3DYes.29" name="How_to_share_home_folders_with_read.2Fwrite_permissions_.28Authentication.3DYes.29">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to share home folders with read/write permissions (Authentication=Yes)
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_install_Samba_Server_for_files.2Ffolders_sharing_service" title="">
         #How to install Samba Server for files/folders sharing service
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       cp /etc/samba/smb.conf /etc/samba/smb.conf_backup
gedit /etc/samba/smb.conf
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Find this line
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       ...
;  security = user
...
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Replace with the following lines
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       security = user
  username map = /etc/samba/smbusers
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Save the edited file
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_add.2Fedit.2Fdelete_network_users" title="">
         #How to add/edit/delete network users
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       testparm
/etc/init.d/smb restart
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_share_home_folders_with_read_only_permission_.28Authentication.3DYes.29" name="How_to_share_home_folders_with_read_only_permission_.28Authentication.3DYes.29">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to share home folders with read only permission (Authentication=Yes)
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_install_Samba_Server_for_files.2Ffolders_sharing_service" title="">
         #How to install Samba Server for files/folders sharing service
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       cp /etc/samba/smb.conf /etc/samba/smb.conf_backup
gedit /etc/samba/smb.conf
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Find this line
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       ...
;  security = user
...
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Replace with the following lines
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       security = user
  username map = /etc/samba/smbusers
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Find this line
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       [homes]
	comment = Home Directories
	browseable = no
	writeable = yes
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Replace with the following lines
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       [homes]
	comment = Home Directories
	browseable = yes
	writeable = no
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Save the edited file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       testparm
/etc/init.d/smb restart
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_share_group_folders_with_read_only_permission_.28Authentication.3DYes.29" name="How_to_share_group_folders_with_read_only_permission_.28Authentication.3DYes.29">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to share group folders with read only permission (Authentication=Yes)
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_install_Samba_Server_for_files.2Ffolders_sharing_service" title="">
         #How to install Samba Server for files/folders sharing service
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       mkdir /home/group
chmod 777 /home/group/
cp /etc/samba/smb.conf /etc/samba/smb.conf_backup
gedit /etc/samba/smb.conf
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Find this line
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       ...
;  security = user
...
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Replace with the following lines
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       security = user
 username map = /etc/samba/smbusers
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Append the following lines at the end of file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       [Group]
  comment = Group Folder
  path = /home/group
  public = yes
  writable = no
  valid users = system_username1 system_username2
  create mask = 0700
  directory mask = 0700
  force user = nobody
  force group = nogroup
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Save the edited file
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_add.2Fedit.2Fdelete_network_users" title="">
         #How to add/edit/delete network users
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       testparm
/etc/init.d/smb restart
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_share_group_folders_with_read.2Fwrite_permissions_.28Authentication.3DYes.29" name="How_to_share_group_folders_with_read.2Fwrite_permissions_.28Authentication.3DYes.29">

      <a id="SSH" name="SSH">
      </a>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        SSH
       </span>
      </h2>
      <a id="How_to_SSH_into_remote_Fedora_machine" name="How_to_SSH_into_remote_Fedora_machine">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to SSH into remote Fedora machine
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <i>
         e.g. Assumed that remote Fedora machine have installed SSH Server service and firewall allows to connect to it
        </i>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        <i>
         Remote Fedora machine: 192.168.0.1
        </i>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <pre>
       ssh username@192.168.0.1
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_copy_files.2Ffolders_from_remote_Fedora_machine_into_local_machine_.28scp.29" name="How_to_copy_files.2Ffolders_from_remote_Fedora_machine_into_local_machine_.28scp.29">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to copy files/folders from remote Fedora machine into local machine (scp)
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <i>
         e.g. Assumed that remote Fedora machine have installed SSH Server service and firewall allows to connect to it
        </i>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        <i>
         Remote Fedora machine: 192.168.0.1
        </i>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        <i>
         Remote files/folders location: /home/username/remotefile.txt
        </i>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        <i>
         Local machine save location: . (current directory)
        </i>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <pre>
       scp -r username@192.168.0.1:/home/username/remotefile.txt .
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_copy_files.2Ffolders_from_local_machine_into_remote_Fedora_machine_.28scp.29" name="How_to_copy_files.2Ffolders_from_local_machine_into_remote_Fedora_machine_.28scp.29">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to copy files/folders from local machine into remote Fedora machine (scp)
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <i>
         e.g. Assumed that remote Fedora machine have installed SSH Server service and firewall allows to connect to it
        </i>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        <i>
         Local files/folders location: localfile.txt
        </i>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        <i>
         Remote Fedora machine: 192.168.0.1
        </i>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        <i>
         Remote Fedora machine save location: /home/username/
        </i>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <pre>
       scp -r localfile.txt username@192.168.0.1:/home/username/
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_copy_files.2Ffolders_from_remote_Fedora_machine_into_local_machine_.28rsync.29" name="How_to_copy_files.2Ffolders_from_remote_Fedora_machine_into_local_machine_.28rsync.29">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to copy files/folders from remote Fedora machine into local machine (rsync)
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <i>
         e.g. Assumed that remote Fedora machine have installed SSH Server service and firewall allows to connect to it
        </i>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        <i>
         Remote Fedora machine: 192.168.0.1
        </i>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        <i>
         Remote files/folders location: /home/username/remotefile.txt
        </i>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        <i>
         Local machine save location: . (current directory)
        </i>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <pre>
       rsync -v -u -a --delete --rsh=ssh --stats username@192.168.0.1:/home/username/remotefile.txt .
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_copy_files.2Ffolders_from_local_machine_into_remote_Fedora_machine_.28rsync.29" name="How_to_copy_files.2Ffolders_from_local_machine_into_remote_Fedora_machine_.28rsync.29">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to copy files/folders from local machine into remote Fedora machine (rsync)
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <i>
         e.g. Assumed that remote Fedora machine have installed SSH Server service and firewall allows to connect to it
        </i>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        <i>
         Local files/folders location: localfile.txt
        </i>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        <i>
         Remote Fedora machine: 192.168.0.1
        </i>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        <i>
         Remote Fedora machine save location: /home/username/
        </i>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <pre>
       rsync -v -u -a --delete --rsh=ssh --stats localfile.txt username@192.168.0.1:/home/username/
      </pre>

      <a id="Database_Server" name="Database_Server">

      <h2>

        Database Server
       </span>
      </h2>
      <a id="How_to_install_MYSQL_Database_Server" name="How_to_install_MYSQL_Database_Server">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to install MYSQL Database Server
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_add_extra_repositories" title="">
         #How to add extra repositories
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Use
        <i>
         Desktop -&gt; System Settings -&gt; Add/Remove Applications
        </i>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <b>
         or
        </b>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <pre>
       yum -y install mysql
yum -y install mysql-server
yum -y install php-mysql
yum -y install MySQL-python
yum -y install libdbi-dbd-mysql
yum -y install mysql-devel
      </pre>
      <pre>
       /etc/init.d/mysqld start
mysqladmin -u root password new_db_user_password
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_install_MYSQL_Control_Center" name="How_to_install_MYSQL_Control_Center">

       yum -y install mysql-administrator
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Applications -&gt; System Tools -&gt; MySQL Administrator
       </li>
      </ul>
      <a id="Web_Server" name="Web_Server">

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        Web Server
       </span>
      </h2>
      <a id="How_to_install_Web_Server" name="How_to_install_Web_Server">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to install Web Server
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_add_extra_repositories" title="">
         #How to add extra repositories
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       yum -y install httpd
yum -y install mod_ssl
yum -y install httpd-manual
yum -y install mod_perl
yum -y install mod_auth_mysql
yum -y install crypto-utils
yum -y install mod_python
/etc/init.d/httpd start
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a class="external free" href="http://localhost" title="http://localhost">
         http://localhost
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <a id="How_to_install_PHP_Web_Server" name="How_to_install_PHP_Web_Server">

      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">

yum -y install php-mysql

      </pre>
      <a id="Apache_tips" name="Apache_tips">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        Apache tips
       </span>
      </h4>
      <p>
       Remove your server's signature
      </p>
      <pre>
       gedit /etc/httpd/conf/httpd.conf
      </pre>
      <p>
       find the line  "ServerSignature"
      </p>
      <p>
       Change "ServerSignature on" to
      </p>
      <pre>
       <b>
        ServerSignature off
       </b>
      </pre>
      <ol>
       <li>
        Underneath add this line:
       </li>
      </ol>
      <pre>
       ServerTokens ProductOnly
      </pre>
      <p>
       Save and close the text editer
      </p>
      <p>
       restart apache
      </p>
      <pre>
       /etc/rc.d/init.d/httpd restart
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_map_URLs_to_folders_outside_.2Fvar.2Fwww.2F" name="How_to_map_URLs_to_folders_outside_.2Fvar.2Fwww.2F">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to map URLs to folders outside /var/www/
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_install_Web_Server" title="">
         #How to install Web Server
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       gedit /etc/httpd/conf.d/alias
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Insert the following lines into the new file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       Alias /URL-path /location_of_folder/
      </pre>
      <pre>
       &lt;Directory /location_of_folder/&gt;
  Options Indexes FollowSymLinks
  AllowOverride All
  Order allow,deny
  Allow from all
&lt;/Directory&gt;
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Save the edited file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       /etc/init.d/httpd restart
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a class="external free" href="http://localhost/URL-path" title="http://localhost/URL-path">
         http://localhost/URL-path
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <a id="How_to_change_the_default_port_number_for_Apache_HTTP_Server" name="How_to_change_the_default_port_number_for_Apache_HTTP_Server">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to change the default port number for Apache HTTP Server
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_install_Web_Server" title="">
         #How to install Web Server
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <i>
         e.g. Assumed that new port number is 78
        </i>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <pre>
       cp /etc/httpd/ports.conf /etc/httpd/ports.conf_backup
gedit /etc/httpd/ports.conf
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Find this line
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       Listen 80
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Replace with the following line
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       Listen 78
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Save the edited file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       /etc/init.d/httpd restart
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a class="external free" href="http://localhost:78" title="http://localhost:78">
         http://localhost:78
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <a id="How_to_parse_RSS_into_PHP_for_Apache_HTTP_Server" name="How_to_parse_RSS_into_PHP_for_Apache_HTTP_Server">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to parse RSS into PHP for Apache HTTP Server
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_install_Web_Server" title="">
         #How to install Web Server
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_install_PHP_for_Web_Server" title="">
         #How to install PHP for Web Server
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <i>
         e.g. Assumed that RSS is DistroWatch.com - News
        </i>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <pre>
       wget -c
       <a class="external free" href="http://easylinux.info/uploads/magpierss-0.71.1.tar.gz" title="http://easylinux.info/uploads/magpierss-0.71.1.tar.gz">
        http://easylinux.info/uploads/magpierss-0.71.1.tar.gz
       </a>
       mkdir /var/www/feeds
tar zxvf magpierss-0.71.1.tar.gz -C /var/www/feeds/
mv /var/www/feeds/magpierss-0.71.1/* /var/www/feeds/
rm -fr /var/www/feeds/magpierss-0.71.1/
chown -R www-data:root /var/www/feeds/
gedit /var/www/feeds/index.php
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Insert the following lines into the new file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       &lt;!DOCTYPE html PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD XHTML 1.0 Strict//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/xhtml1/DTD/xhtml1-strict.dtd"&gt;
 
 &lt;html xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml" lang="en" xml:lang="en"&gt;
 
 &lt;head&gt;
 
 &lt;title&gt;DistroWatch.com - News&lt;/title&gt;
 
 &lt;meta http-equiv="Content-Type" content="text/html; charset=iso-8859-1"/&gt;
 
 &lt;style type="text/css"&gt;
 /*&lt;![CDATA[*/
 /* 
 DEFAULT TAG STYLES
 */
 
 body {
  background: #ffffff;
  margin-left: 20px;
  font-family: bitstream vera sans,sans-serif;
  font-size: 9pt;
 }
 
 h1 {
  font-family: luxi sans,sans-serif;
  font-size: 15pt;
 }
 
 /*]]&gt;*/
 &lt;/style&gt;
 
 &lt;/head&gt;
  
 &lt;body&gt;
 
 &lt;?php

 require_once 'rss_fetch.inc';
 error_reporting(E_ERROR);
 
 $url = 'http://distrowatch.com/news/dw.xml';
 $rss = fetch_rss($url);
 
 if ($rss) {
 
  echo "&lt;h1&gt;";
  echo "&lt;a href=$url&gt;", $rss-&gt;channel[title], "&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;";
  echo "&lt;/h1&gt;";
 
  foreach ($rss-&gt;items as $item ) {
   $url = $item[link];
   $title = $item[title];
   $description = $item[description];
   echo "&lt;li&gt;";
   echo "&lt;b&gt;Topic:&lt;/b&gt; &lt;a href=$url&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;$title&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;";
   echo "$description&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;";
   echo "&lt;/li&gt;";
  }
 
 }
 else {
  echo "&lt;a href=$url&gt;", $url, "&lt;/a&gt; - Server Down!&lt;br/&gt;";
 }
 
 ?&gt;
 
 &lt;/body&gt;
 
 &lt;/html&gt;
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Save the edited file
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="external free" href="http://localhost/feeds/index.php" title="http://localhost/feeds/index.php">
         http://localhost/feeds/index.php
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <a id="FTP_Server" name="FTP_Server">
      </a>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        FTP Server
       </span>
      </h2>
      <a id="How_to_install_FTP_Server_for_File_Transfer_service" name="How_to_install_FTP_Server_for_File_Transfer_service">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to install FTP Server for File Transfer service
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_add_extra_repositories" title="">
         #How to add extra repositories
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       yum -y install proftpd
/etc/init.d/proftpd start
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_configure_FTP_Server_to_allow_anonymous_FTP_user_to_read_only" name="How_to_configure_FTP_Server_to_allow_anonymous_FTP_user_to_read_only">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to configure FTP Server to allow anonymous FTP user to read only
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_install_FTP_Server_for_File_Transfer_service" title="">
         #How to install FTP Server for File Transfer service
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       cp /etc/proftpd.conf /etc/proftpd.conf_backup
gedit /etc/proftpd.conf
      </pre>
      <p>
       <br/>
      </p>
      <p>
       <br/>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Append the following lines at the end of file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       &lt;Anonymous ~ftp&gt;
 User            ftp
 Group            nogroup
 UserAlias          anonymous ftp
 DirFakeUser on ftp
 DirFakeGroup on ftp
 RequireValidShell      off
 MaxClients         10
 DisplayLogin        welcome.msg
 DisplayFirstChdir      .message
 &lt;Directory *&gt;
  &lt;Limit WRITE&gt;
   DenyAll
  &lt;/Limit&gt;
 &lt;/Directory&gt;
&lt;/Anonymous&gt;
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Save the edited file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       /etc/init.d/proftpd restart
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_configure_FTP_Server_to_allow_anonymous_FTP_user_to_read.2Fwrite" name="How_to_configure_FTP_Server_to_allow_anonymous_FTP_user_to_read.2Fwrite">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to configure FTP Server to allow anonymous FTP user to read/write
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_install_FTP_Server_for_File_Transfer_service" title="">
         #How to install FTP Server for File Transfer service
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       cp /etc/proftpd.conf /etc/proftpd.conf_backup
gedit /etc/proftpd.conf
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Append the following lines at the end of file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       &lt;Anonymous ~ftp&gt;
 User            ftp
 Group            nogroup
 UserAlias          anonymous ftp
 DirFakeUser on ftp
 DirFakeGroup on ftp
 RequireValidShell      off
 MaxClients         10
 DisplayLogin        welcome.msg
 DisplayFirstChdir      .message
&lt;/Anonymous&gt;
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Save the edited file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       /etc/init.d/proftpd restart
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_map_anonymous_FTP_user_to_folders_outside_.2Fhome.2Fftp.2F" name="How_to_map_anonymous_FTP_user_to_folders_outside_.2Fhome.2Fftp.2F">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to map anonymous FTP user to folders outside /home/ftp/
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_install_FTP_Server_for_File_Transfer_service" title="">
         #How to install FTP Server for File Transfer service
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       cp /etc/proftpd.conf /etc/proftpd.conf_backup
gedit /etc/proftpd.conf
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Append the following lines at the end of file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       &lt;Anonymous /location_of_folder/&gt;
 User            ftp
 Group            nogroup
 UserAlias          anonymous ftp
 DirFakeUser on ftp
 DirFakeGroup on ftp
 RequireValidShell      off
 MaxClients         10
 DisplayLogin        welcome.msg
 DisplayFirstChdir      .message
 &lt;Directory *&gt;
  &lt;Limit WRITE&gt;
   DenyAll
  &lt;/Limit&gt;
 &lt;/Directory&gt;
&lt;/Anonymous&gt;
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Save the edited file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       /etc/init.d/proftpd restart
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_change_the_default_port_number_for_FTP_Server" name="How_to_change_the_default_port_number_for_FTP_Server">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to change the default port number for FTP Server
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#How_to_install_FTP_Server_for_File_Transfer_service" title="">
         #How to install FTP Server for File Transfer service
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <i>
         e.g. Assumed that new port number is 77
        </i>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <pre>
       cp /etc/proftpd.conf /etc/proftpd.conf_backup
gedit /etc/proftpd.conf
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Find this line
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       Port              21
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Replace with the following line
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       Port              77
      </pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Save the edited file
       </li>
      </ul>
      <pre>
       /etc/init.d/proftpd restart
      </pre>
      <a id="How_to_ftp_into_remote_Fedora_machine_via_Windows_machine" name="How_to_ftp_into_remote_Fedora_machine_via_Windows_machine">
      </a>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline">
        How to ftp into remote Fedora machine via Windows machine
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Read
        <a href="#General_Notes" title="">
         #General Notes
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <i>
         e.g. Assumed that remote Fedora machine have installed FTP Server service
        </i>
       </dd>
       <dd>
        <i>
         Read
         <a href="#How_to_install_FTP_Server_for_File_Transfer_service" title="">
          #How to install FTP Server for File Transfer service
         </a>
        </i>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Download FileZilla:
        <a class="external text" href="http://prdownloads.sourceforge.net/filezilla/FileZilla_2_2_17_setup.exe?download" title="http://prdownloads.sourceforge.net/filezilla/FileZilla_2_2_17_setup.exe?download">
         Here
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
